<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1134653256">.mw-parser-output .side-box{margin:4px 0;box-sizing:border-box;border:1px solid #aaa;font-size:88%;line-height:1.25em;background-color:#f9f9f9;display:flow-root}.mw-parser-output .side-box-abovebelow,.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{padding:0.25em 0.9em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-image{padding:2px 0 2px 0.9em;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-imageright{padding:2px 0.9em 2px 0;text-align:center}@media(min-width:500px){.mw-parser-output .side-box-flex{display:flex;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{flex:1}}@media(min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .side-box{width:238px}.mw-parser-output .side-box-right{clear:right;float:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-left{margin-right:1em}}</style><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1092331828">@media(min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .contains-special-characters{width:22em}}</style><div class="side-box metadata side-box-right contains-special-characters noprint selfref"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1126788409">
<div class="side-box-flex">
<div class="side-box-image"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg/40px-Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="10" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg/60px-Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg/80px-Thai_Alphabet_Sample.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></div>
<div class="side-box-text plainlist"><b>This article contains <a href="/wiki/Thai_language" title="Thai language">Thai text</a>.</b> Without proper <a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support_(Indic)" title="Help:Multilingual support (Indic)">rendering support</a>, you may see <a href="/wiki/Specials_(Unicode_block)#Replacement_character" title="Specials (Unicode block)">question marks, boxes, or other symbols</a>&#32;instead of <a href="/wiki/Thai_script" title="Thai script">Thai script</a>.</div></div>
</div>
<p><b>Nichkhun Buck Horvejkul</b><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> (<a href="/wiki/Thai_language" title="Thai language">Thai</a>: <span lang="th">นิชคุณ หรเวชกุล</span>; <small><a href="/wiki/Royal_Thai_General_System_of_Transcription" title="Royal Thai General System of Transcription">RTGS</a>:&#160;</small><span title="Royal Thai General System of Transcription"><span style="font-style: inherit" lang="th-Latn"><i>Nitchakhun Horawetchakun</i></span></span>; born June 24, 1988), better known mononymously as <b>Nichkhun</b> (<a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a>: <span lang="ko">닉쿤</span>), is a <a href="/wiki/Thai_Americans" title="Thai Americans">Thai American</a><sup id="cite_ref-travel.cnn.com_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-travel.cnn.com-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> rapper, singer, songwriter, actor and model who is currently based in South Korea as a member of the South Korean boy band <a href="/wiki/2PM" title="2PM">2PM</a>.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Nichkhun was born in <a href="/wiki/Rancho_Cucamonga,_California" title="Rancho Cucamonga, California">Rancho Cucamonga, California</a>, U.S. to <a href="/wiki/Thai_Chinese" title="Thai Chinese">Thai Chinese</a> parents and was raised in Thailand.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span style="white-space: nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot"><span title="&#160;Dead link tagged December 2022">dead link</span></a></i>&#93;</span></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hainan_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hainan-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> His mother's family is from <a href="/wiki/Hainan" title="Hainan">Hainan</a>, and he has said that he has extended family and distant ancestors from <a href="/wiki/Guangzhou" title="Guangzhou">Guangzhou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-hainan_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hainan-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nickhun's mother, Yenjit Horvejkul (née Mekworewut), is the chief executive officer of a Thai pharmaceutical company, Union Medical, established in 1976, which acts as an importer and distributor.<sup id="cite_ref-soompi.com_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soompi.com-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (June 2018)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> He comes from a wealthy background, which earned him the nickname "Thai Prince" in South Korea.<sup id="cite_ref-soompi.com_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soompi.com-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun has one older brother, Nichan Bert (born September 11, 1986),<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and two younger sisters, Nichthima Yanin (born July 22, 1990)<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and Nachjaree (Chereen) (born October 20, 1994). At the age of five, he moved to Thailand from the United States with his family and studied at Dhepkanjana School and Tangpiroondham School. At the age of twelve, he studied at <a href="/wiki/Wanganui_Collegiate_School" class="mw-redirect" title="Wanganui Collegiate School">Wanganui Collegiate School</a> in New Zealand for a year and a half and moved back to the United States to finish his schooling at <a href="/wiki/Los_Osos_High_School" title="Los Osos High School">Los Osos High School</a> in Rancho Cucamonga, California. He was scouted by a scout manager of <a href="/wiki/JYP_Entertainment" title="JYP Entertainment">JYP Entertainment</a> at the Los Angeles Korean Music Festival.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After passing an audition hosted by JYP Entertainment, he signed a ten-year contract with the company but later re-signed an eight-year contract, not including training, and was brought to South Korea in 2006 as a trainee, being put into a class of 24 other students. <a href="/wiki/Park_Jin-young" title="Park Jin-young">Park Jin-young</a> informed him that he was required to learn how to sing and dance, learn <a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a> and <a href="/wiki/Standard_Chinese" title="Standard Chinese">Mandarin Chinese</a>, and bulk up. He speaks fluent Thai, English, Korean, Japanese and basic Chinese. He first appeared through <a href="/wiki/Mnet_(TV_channel)" title="Mnet (TV channel)">Mnet</a>'s <i>Hot Blood</i>, a program that showed the intense physical training that 13 male trainees had to go through for the opportunity to debut in either a four-member ballad group (<a href="/wiki/2AM_(band)" title="2AM (band)">2AM</a>) or a seven-member dance group (<a href="/wiki/2PM" title="2PM">2PM</a>) under JYP Entertainment.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span style="white-space: nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot"><span title="&#160;Dead link tagged December 2022">dead link</span></a></i>&#93;</span></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career">Career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2PM">2PM</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2PM">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1033289096">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2PM" title="2PM">2PM</a></div>
<p>On September 4, 2008, Nichkhun debuted as part of 2PM in their first single "10 Points out of 10 Points" (<a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a>: <span lang="ko">"10점 만점에 10점"</span>) from their single album "<a href="/wiki/10_Out_of_10_(2PM_song)" title="10 Out of 10 (2PM song)">Hottest Time of the Day</a>". They have released five studio albums in Korea and four studio albums in Japan.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Solo_activities">Solo activities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Solo activities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.932015:_Host.2C_variety_show.2C_designer_and_acting_roles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–2015:_Host,_variety_show,_designer_and_acting_roles">2010–2015: Host, variety show, designer and acting roles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2010–2015: Host, variety show, designer and acting roles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Nichkhun_in_July_2011_(2).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg/170px-Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="295" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg/255px-Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg/340px-Nichkhun_in_July_2011_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="481" data-file-height="836" /></a><figcaption>Nichkhun in July 2011</figcaption></figure>
<p>Nichkhun was one of the hosts for the Korean Music Wave in Bangkok in 2010, 2011, and 2013. In 2010, along with <a href="/wiki/Ok_Taec-yeon" title="Ok Taec-yeon">Taecyeon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yoon_Eun-hye" title="Yoon Eun-hye">Yoon Eun-hye</a>, Nichkhun played one of the main characters in a 12-minute music video drama for <a href="/wiki/Cass_(beer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cass (beer)">Cass Beer</a>, which was released on February 8.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He also hosted JYP's talent competition <i>Superstar Survival</i>. In June 2010, he was cast in the second season of the variety show <i><a href="/wiki/We_Got_Married_(season_2)" title="We Got Married (season 2)">We Got Married</a></i>, pairing up with <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Song" title="Victoria Song">Victoria</a> of <a href="/wiki/F(x)_(band)" class="mw-redirect" title="F(x) (band)">f(x)</a>. The couple, known as <a href="/wiki/Khuntoria" class="mw-redirect" title="Khuntoria">Khuntoria</a>, was featured on the show leaving in September 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> In 2011, Nichkhun appeared in the music video of the single "Touch (觸動)" by Taiwanese <a href="/wiki/Mandopop" title="Mandopop">Mandopop</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Will_Pan" title="Will Pan">Will Pan</a>, which premiered on January 31. He also starred in the Japanese live-adaptation film of <i><a href="/wiki/Ouran_High_School_Host_Club" title="Ouran High School Host Club">Ouran High School Host Club</a></i> as Lawrence, the president of a Singaporean corporation.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2012, Nichkhun starred in a Thai movie for the first time <i><a href="/wiki/Seven_Something" title="Seven Something">Seven Something</a></i> and took on the role of a young marathon runner. The romantic anthology film was produced by Thailand's film studio and distributor GTH and released on July 26, 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In 2013, he filmed for the Chinese TV series <i><a href="/wiki/One_and_a_Half_Summer" title="One and a Half Summer">One and a Half Summer</a></i>, where he plays the lead character. The series aired between June and July 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun was appointed “Friend of UNICEF” on April 9, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Since then, he has participated in several field visits to promote children's rights and increase awareness of children's issues. Nichkhun has played an important role in helping UNICEF to mobilize funds to help children in Thailand and across the world, especially during emergency situations. As a result, in March 2015, Nichkhun has been awarded a recognition plaque from UNICEF Thailand for his dedication and hard work.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2014, Japanese network NTV's <a href="/wiki/Kindaichi_Shounen_no_Jikenbo" class="mw-redirect" title="Kindaichi Shounen no Jikenbo">Kindaichi Shounen no Jikenbo</a> mystery drama special was broadcast on January 4. Nichkhun took on the role of a young student who was involved in a serial murder case set in the jungles of Malaysia.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Nichkhun started filming for his Chinese drama <i>Looking for Aurora</i> in June. The drama held its production press conference in Shenzhen on August 28.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> In August, Nichkhun also debuted as a designer<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> and released bag collection in collaboration with Korean fashion brand ‘rosa.K.’ The ‘ROSA.K x Nichkhun Collaboration’ consisted of three different lines: Dustin, Lawnick, and Dave, and the showcase was held on August 26, 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Nichkhun teamed up with <a href="/wiki/CNBLUE" title="CNBLUE">CNBLUE</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jung_Yong-hwa" title="Jung Yong-hwa">Jung Yong-hwa</a>, <a href="/wiki/B1A4" title="B1A4">B1A4</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Baro_(singer)" title="Baro (singer)">Baro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Infinite_(band)" class="mw-redirect" title="Infinite (band)">Infinite</a>'s <a href="/wiki/L_(South_Korean_singer)" class="mw-redirect" title="L (South Korean singer)">L</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Winner_(band)" title="Winner (band)">Winner</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Song_Min-ho" class="mw-redirect" title="Song Min-ho">Mino</a> for project group Lucky Boys (Super 5) for the 2014 <a href="/wiki/SBS_Gayo_Daejun" class="mw-redirect" title="SBS Gayo Daejun">SBS Gayo Daejun</a>. Nichkhun and Baro also hosted the show.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2015, Nichkhun made a cameo appearance in the Chinese movie <i>Forever Young</i>, starring <a href="/wiki/Li_Yi_Feng" class="mw-redirect" title="Li Yi Feng">Li Yi Feng</a> and Zhang Hui We,<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> and a Thai movie <i>Touch the Sky - Chalui</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun also became a mentor on a Chinese music reality show <i>Youth Trainee</i> on Zhejiang Television.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.932020:_Acting_roles.2C_host.2C_first_mini_album_and_solo_concert"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–2020:_Acting_roles,_host,_first_mini_album_and_solo_concert">2016–2020: Acting roles, host, first mini album and solo concert</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2016–2020: Acting roles, host, first mini album and solo concert">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In 2016, Nichkhun and actor <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jung-jin" title="Lee Jung-jin">Lee Jung-jin</a> released a travel essay and photobook called '여행, 바람을 품은 지도' (Journey, Map that embraces the Wind) on May 3. The photos in the book were taken during their trip to Hawaii, USA.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2017, Nichkhun joined the main cast of a Korean series for the first time on JTBC's <i>Magic School</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> In September, Nichkhun announced his first-ever solo Asia fan meeting tour since making his debut in 2008. His fan meetings 'Nichkhun (of 2PM) 1st Asia Fan Meeting Tour &lt;Khunvitation&gt;' were held in Tokyo and Osaka, Japan between November 29–30 and December 13–14, respectively. His fan meeting &lt;Khunvitation&gt; in Seoul, South Korea, was held on December 3.<sup id="cite_ref-https_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-https-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In 2018, Nichkhun continued his fan meeting tour in Thailand and China. Nichkhun focused on his solo activities while some 2PM members served in the military.<sup id="cite_ref-https_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-https-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> His Thai movie <i>Brother of the Year</i> ranked No. 1 in Thai box offices and became the second highest-grossing Thai movie in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun released his first solo mini album in Japan on December 19, 2018. Titled <i>Me</i>, the album contains 8 tracks, including songs like "Lucky Charm", "Endearing", and "Mars". Nichkhun participated in composing and writing the lyrics for every song on the album. Prior to the release of his album, Nichkhun held his first solo concert "NICHKHUN (From 2PM) Premium Solo Concert 2018 HOME" in Osaka on November 23 and 24, and in Tokyo from December 20 to 22.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Nichkhun's Chinese web drama <i>Shall We Fall in Love</i> (勇往直前恋上你) premiered on Tencent on December 27, 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nichkhun traveled to work in several countries in 2018, especially to shoot for travel and food programs, including JTBC and Thailand's <a href="/wiki/One_31" title="One 31">ONE31</a> <i>The Team Chef</i><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> and JTBC <i>Let's Eat Dinner Together</i><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> in South Korea, tvN <i>Galileo: Awakened Universe</i><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> in the United States, tvN Asia <i>One Night Food Trip – International Edition 2</i><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> in the Philippines, tvN Asia <i>Wok The World</i><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> in Singapore, and The Tourism Authority of Thailand <i>Experience Thailand and More</i><sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> in Thailand, Myanmar, and Indonesia.
</p><p>In 2019, Nichkhun released his solo album <i>Me</i> in South Korea on February 18.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> The album was available for streaming in South Korea, China, and Thailand. A special song called "Umbrella" dedicated to his fans was released in five different languages Japanese, Korean, Chinese, Thai, and English.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun held his solo concerts 'Home' in Seoul on May 11 and 12. He also held his encore concerts called 'Nichkhun Solo Concert 'Home' Encore in Japan ~Sweet 624~' on June 27 and 28 in Tokyo.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Reliable sources"><span title="The material near this tag may rely on an unreliable source. (December 2022)">unreliable source?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> On July 27, Nichkhun held his solo concert called Nichkhun Solo Concert 'Home' in Bangkok with Dr.Jill in Thailand.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun started filming for Viu Original Thai series called <i>My Bubble Tea</i> in July 2019<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and a Thai horror movie, <a href="/wiki/CJ_Major_Entertainment" title="CJ Major Entertainment">CJ Major Entertainment</a>'s <i>Cracked</i> in August 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On October 28, Nichkhun announced the release of his second mini album in Japan titled 'Story of...' and solo concerts called "NICHKHUN (From 2PM) Premium Solo Concert 2019-2020 'Story of...'" <sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On December 19, his album 'Story of...' was released in digital format simultaneously in Japan and Korea. The physical format of the album was released on December 25.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun held his solo concerts 'Story of...' in Osaka on December 26 and 27.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2020, Nichkhun continued his tour "NICHKHUN (From 2PM) Premium Solo Concert 2019-2020 'Story of...'" in Tokyo on January 6 and 7.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On May 22, 2020, his Thai drama <i>My Bubble Tea</i> alongside Thai stars Mean Phiravich and Manasaporn Chanchalerm aired on Viu. The <a href="/wiki/Viu_(streaming_media)" class="mw-redirect" title="Viu (streaming media)">Viu Original</a> drama revolves around Manasaporn's character who concocts a special tea so that she can make her boss (played by Nichkhun) fall in love with her.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On September 21, 2020, Nichkhun and <a href="/wiki/Day6" title="Day6">Day6</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jae_Park" title="Jae Park">Jae Park</a> took on role as a member of crime-fighting boyband "4 2 Sing" in season three of <i><a href="/wiki/Big_Hero_6:_The_Series" title="Big Hero 6: The Series">Big Hero 6: The Series</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Nichkhun played twins Dae and Hyun-ki, one half of the boy band "4 2 Sing", while Jae Park played another set of twins, Kwang-sun and Ye Joon, also "4 2 Sing" members.
</p><p>On October 25, 2020, Nichkhun and 2019 Miss Korea Kim Se-yeon hosted "Asia Contents Awards 2020".<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2021.E2.80.93present:_Upcoming_Hollywood_film"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2021–present:_Upcoming_Hollywood_film">2021–present: Upcoming Hollywood film</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2021–present: Upcoming Hollywood film">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In 2021, Nichkhun and <a href="/wiki/Hwang_Chan-sung" title="Hwang Chan-sung">Hwang Chan-sung</a> made special cameo appearances in <a href="/wiki/Vincenzo_(TV_series)" title="Vincenzo (TV series)"><i>Vincenzo</i></a> to support their bandmate <a href="/wiki/Ok_Taec-yeon" title="Ok Taec-yeon">Ok Taec-yeon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nichkhun will be starring in an upcoming Hollywood film, <i>Hong Kong Love Story</i>, a romantic comedy directed by <a href="/wiki/Keoni_Waxman" title="Keoni Waxman">Keoni Waxman</a>. Nichkhun has been cast alongside <a href="/wiki/Byron_Mann" title="Byron Mann">Byron Mann</a>, Rayssa Bratillieri, Dominika Kachlik, and <a href="/wiki/Kenneth_Tsang" title="Kenneth Tsang">Kenneth Tsang</a>. Based on real events, <i>Hong Kong Love Story</i> follows Nichkhun and Byron Mann as the sons of wealthy families who go to Hong Kong and experience various incidents that teach them the meaning of love and friendship.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> The film was renamed <i>The Modelizer</i> and will be released through <a href="/wiki/Vertical_Entertainment" title="Vertical Entertainment">Vertical Entertainment</a> on July 14, 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As a male citizen of Thailand, he was subject to the military draft lottery in 2009 and subsequently received an exemption from military service.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On July 24, 2012, Nichkhun was involved in a vehicular collision with a motorcyclist in Gangnam. It was reported that the singer had been <a href="/wiki/Driving_under_the_influence" title="Driving under the influence">driving under the influence</a> of alcohol when he crashed into a motorcycle. His BAC measured at 0.056%, thus his license was suspended. Nichkhun personally apologized for his recent drunk driving incident, resulting in him taking a hiatus from the entertainment industry.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Discography">Discography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Discography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Promotional_songs">Promotional songs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Promotional songs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soundtrack_appearances">Soundtrack appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nichkhun&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Soundtrack appearances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>2011: "My Valentine" (with <a href="/wiki/Park_Jin-young" title="Park Jin-young">J.Y. Park</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Ok_Taec-yeon" title="Ok Taec-yeon">Taecyeon</a>), <i><a href="/wiki/Dream_High" title="Dream High">Dream High</a> OST</i></li>
<li>2012: "Let It Rain", <i><a href="/wiki/One_and_a_Half_Summer" title="One and a Half Summer">One and a Half Summer</a> OST</i></li>
<li>2015: "Wan Nun Wan Nee Wan Nhai" (วันนั้น วันนี้ วันไหน) (featuring <a href="/wiki/Ok_Taec-yeon" title="Ok Taec-yeon">Taecyeon</a>), <i>Touch the Sky - Chalui OST</i></li>
<li>2018: "Fall in Love With You" (勇往直前恋上你), <i>Shall We Fall in Love? OST</i></li></ul>
